[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability, classified as medium [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseverity by the Jazzer security issue detection system. SSRF vulnerabilities occur [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen an application makes requests to arbitrary destinations based on untrusted [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser input, which can lead to:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltration of sensitive data[0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Network Connection Attempt**: The stack trace shows an attempted HTTPS [0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy for SSRF Vulnerability in TextAndCSVParser[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability in Apache Tika's `TextAndCSVParser` is caused by the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method automatically making network connections to URLs extracted [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom CSV cell content. The vulnerability occurs when:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. A CSV file contains Excel-style `=[0m[1;35mHYPERLINK[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"url"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"name"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` formulas[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method matches these formulas using the `HYPERLINK_PATTERN` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregex[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. After correctly creating an HTML anchor tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it unnecessarily [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m261[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method opens a `URLConnection` and fetches external content [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout any security validation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis behavior is **architecturally flawed** because:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- External URLs in CSV files should be treated as hyperlink references, not [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded documents to fetch[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The URL fetching is automatic and hidden from users[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No security controls exist [0m[1;39m([0m[39mURL validation, allowlists, private IP checks[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It violates the principle of least surprise - users don't expect network [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnections when parsing local files[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing test only expects HTML anchor tag generation, not URL fetching[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Comparison with Correct Implementation[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe Excel parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFExcelExtractorDecorator.extractHyperLinks[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct approach:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Extracts hyperlinks from document metadata[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Renders them as HTML anchor tags[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Does NOT fetch external resources**[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe CSV parser already creates correct HTML anchor tags [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, making the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call redundant and dangerous.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Recommended Fix Strategy[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix: Remove the Dangerous [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Call**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify `TextAndCSVParser.java` at line [0m[1;36m261[0m[39m by removing the call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodule/src/main/java/org/apache/tika/parser/csv/TextAndCSVParser.java`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes Required:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **In the `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m247[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m266[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep lines [0m[1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[39m that create the HTML anchor tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthis is correct behavior[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Remove line [0m[1;36m261[0m[39m** that calls `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This eliminates the SSRF vulnerability entirely[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Remove or deprecate the `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m268[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m285[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since it will no longer be called, this method can be removed[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Alternatively, mark it as deprecated if there's concern about downstream [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely for a private method[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This also removes the unused imports: `java.net.URL` and [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.net.URLConnection`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Modified [0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method should look like:**[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString cellContent, XHTMLContentHandler xhtml,[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         Metadata metadata,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         ParseContext context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException, SAXException [0m[1;39m{[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    Matcher m = [0m[1;35mHYPERLINK_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcellContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        String url = [0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        String name = [0m[1;35mm.group[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mStringUtils.isBlank[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            name = url;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxhtml.startElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"href"[0m[39m, url[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxhtml.endElement[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"a"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m REMOVED: [0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxhtml.characters[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcellContent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mxhtml.endElement[0m[1;39m([0m[39mTD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Complete Security Fix**: Eliminates the SSRF vulnerability entirely by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoving network access[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Maintains Correct Functionality**: The HTML anchor tag generation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already provides the expected output[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: The existing test [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mtestHyperlink[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only verifies [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manchor tag generation, not URL fetching[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Aligns CSV parser behavior with Excel parser and other Tika [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Simplicity**: Minimal code change with maximum security benefit[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: External API remains unchanged; only internal behavior [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis modified[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Performance Improvement**: Removes unnecessary network latency and potential [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimeouts[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it preserves existing functionality:**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- HYPERLINK formulas are still recognized and parsed[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- URLs and display names are correctly extracted[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- HTML anchor tags are properly generated[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Cell content is properly rendered in table cells[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All metadata operations remain intact[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to public APIs or configuration[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How it addresses the evaluation report:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Prevents server-side request forgery[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Stops automatic connections to untrusted destinations[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Eliminates data exfiltration risk[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Prevents exposure of internal services[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ✅ Removes bypassing of firewall protections[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects and mitigation:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **If any code depends on URL fetching**: Highly unlikely since:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is a private method[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The test doesn't verify URL fetching behavior[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Documentation doesn't mention this feature[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Excel parser doesn't have equivalent functionality[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **If embedded document extraction from URLs is desired**: [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This should be an explicit, opt-in feature with proper security controls[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Would require configuration option in `TextAndCSVConfig`[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Would need URL validation, allowlists, and security documentation[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should respect `[0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` control mechanism[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This can be added in a future release if needed, with proper security design[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNot Recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add URL Validation**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` but add security checks[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because**: Adds complexity, still enables SSRF risk, not the intended [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Configuration Toggle**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add option to disable URL fetching[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because**: Makes insecure behavior opt-out instead of fixing it, adds [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintenance burden[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Check [0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mshouldParseEmbedded[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before fetching[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected because**: External URLs shouldn't be treated as embedded documents at[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `TextAndCSVParser.java`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate the `[0m[1;35mprocessCell[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m247[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove line [0m[1;36m261[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Optionally remove the entire `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m268[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m285[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Optionally remove unused imports if `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is removed:[0m                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue identifies a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Apache Tika codebase, specifically in the `TextAndCSVParser` class. The [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability is triggered when the parser attempts to establish a network [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection to an external domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazzer.com:[0m[1;36m443[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m based on untrusted input data, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich could lead to exfiltration of sensitive data or exposure of internal [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mservices.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch was attempted that removes the `processURL` method call and several import [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatements related to URL handling and embedded document extraction. However, the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch resulted in compilation failures because it removed import statements that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare still used by the `processURL` method, which remains in the codebase even [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthough the call to it was removed.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe security issue manifests as a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the following characteristics:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Location**: The issue occurs in the [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.parser.csv.TextAndCSVParser` class, specifically in the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processURL` method at line [0m[1;36m278[0m[39m, which is called from the `processCell` method at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m261[0m[39m, which in turn is called from the `parse` method at line [0m[1;36m211[0m[39m.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Vector**: The stack trace shows that the vulnerability is triggered [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The CSV parser processes cell content[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A URL is detected in the cell content[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The parser attempts to connect to that URL via `processURL`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A socket connection is established through Java's standard URL connection [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Network Activity**: The attempted connection goes through the following Java [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetworking stack:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `java.net.Socket.connect`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - SSL socket implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`sun.security.ssl.SSLSocketImpl`[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - HTTPS client [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`sun.net.www.protocol.https.HttpsClient`[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - HTTP URL connection [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`java.net.www.protocol.http.HttpURLConnection`[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Finally calling `[0m[1;35mgetInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which triggers the actual network request[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Impact**: The SSRF is classified as medium severity, indicating that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted data from parsed CSV files can direct the parser to make arbitrary [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork requests, potentially exposing internal network resources or exfiltrating [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch attempted to address the SSRF vulnerability by making the following [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges to `TextAndCSVParser.java`:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Removed Import Statements**:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `java.net.URL`[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `java.net.URLConnection`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `org.apache.tika.extractor.EmbeddedDocumentExtractor`[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `org.apache.tika.extractor.EmbeddedDocumentUtil`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `org.apache.tika.io.TikaInputStream`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Modified Code Logic**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed the call to `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, metadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m256[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39moriginally line [0m[1;36m261[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code still creates the hyperlink anchor element in the XHTML output but no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlonger processes the URL content[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Incomplete Removal**: The patch removed the imports and the method call but [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdid not remove the `processURL` method itself, which still exists in the codebase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand uses the removed imports.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Compilation Errors[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch resulted in [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m compilation errors, all occurring in the `processURL` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m265[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m272[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Symbol not found errors** for:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `EmbeddedDocumentExtractor` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m265[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `EmbeddedDocumentUtil` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m265[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `URL` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m, appears twice[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `URLConnection` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m270[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `TikaInputStream` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m, appears twice[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese errors indicate that the `processURL` method still exists in the code and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to use these classes, but their import statements were removed.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo achieve a complete understanding and proper fix, the following areas should be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvestigated:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **The processURL Method**: The complete implementation of the `processURL` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod in `TextAndCSVParser.java` needs to be examined to understand:[0m               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **URL Detection Logic**: The code at line [0m[1;36m253[0m[39m that determines whether cell [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Parser Configuration**: Examining the parser's configuration options:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are existing settings to control URL processing[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How the parser is typically configured in production environments[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - What the default behavior should be regarding external resource access[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Related Test Cases**: Investigation of existing test cases for [0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m264[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35massertNotContained[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"HYPERLINK"[0m[39m, xml[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m265[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtika-parsers/tika-parsers-standard/tika-parsers-standard-modules/tika-parser-text-m[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39module/src/test/resources/test-documents/testCSV_hyperlink.csv:[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m7[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m:name,number[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m2:ca[0m[39mt,[0m[1;36m10[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m3:d[0m[39mog,[0m[1;36m15[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m:jaguar,[0m[1;36m23[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m5:a[0m[39mntelope,[0m[1;36m43[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m:[0m[32m"=HYPERLINK[0m[32m([0m[32m"[0m[32m"https://tika.apache.org"[0m[32m","[0m[32m"tika"[0m[32m"[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m100[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m7:e[0m[39mlephant,[0m[1;36m1[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code snippets, I can identify the root cause and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproper fix:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SSRF Vulnerability**: The `processURL` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m268[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m285[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m automatically [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopens network connections to URLs extracted from CSV cell content, which is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted user input[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Incomplete Previous Patch**: The last patch removed imports and the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`processURL` call but left the `processURL` method definition intact, causing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors because the method still references the removed imports[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Inconsistent Behavior**: TextAndCSVParser is the only Tika parser that [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mautomatically fetches URL content from hyperlinks - other parsers [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mXSSFExcelExtractorDecorator, AbstractOOXMLExtractor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m only generate anchor tags [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout fetching content[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **HYPERLINK Pattern Detection**: The regex pattern at lines [0m[1;36m104[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m105[0m[39m must remain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto detect Excel-style hyperlink formulas[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Anchor Tag Generation**: Lines [0m[1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[39m in `processCell` must remain to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgenerate HTML anchor tags[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: The `testHyperlink` test only validates anchor tag [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgeneration, not URL fetching[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Remove the processURL method entirely**[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete lines [0m[1;36m268[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m285[0m[39m which contain the entire `processURL` method definition[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is the root cause of both the SSRF vulnerability and the compilation errors[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove the call to processURL**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete line [0m[1;36m261[0m[39m in the `processCell` method: `[0m[1;35mprocessURL[0m[1;39m([0m[39murl, name, xhtml, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata, context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This was already attempted in the previous patch but needs to be reapplied[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove unused imports**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m25[0m[39m: `import java.net.URL;`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m: `import java.net.URLConnection;`[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m: `import org.apache.tika.extractor.EmbeddedDocumentExtractor;`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m: `import org.apache.tika.extractor.EmbeddedDocumentUtil;`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m52[0m[39m: `import org.apache.tika.io.TikaInputStream;`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove line [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m: `import org.apache.tika.utils.ExceptionUtils;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly used by [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessURL for exception handling[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Verify preserved functionality**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `processCell` method will still:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Detect HYPERLINK patterns via regex [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m252[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Extract URL and display name [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m253[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m256[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Generate HTML anchor tags [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m258[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m260[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Handle non-hyperlink cell content [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m262[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m263[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why this is the optimal approach:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Complete Security Fix**: Removes all network connection code, completely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating the SSRF vulnerability at its source[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Resolves Compilation Errors**: By removing both the method definition and its [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimports, there are no orphaned references[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Maintains Backward Compatibility**: The `testHyperlink` test only validates [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manchor tag generation, which is preserved. No tests validate URL fetching behavior.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Aligns with Tika Patterns**: Matches how other Tika parsers [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mXSSFExcelExtractorDecorator, AbstractOOXMLExtractor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m handle hyperlinks - they [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgenerate anchor tags but don't fetch content[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Principle of Least Privilege**: URLs in document content should be treated as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmetadata/links, not as embedded documents to automatically fetch[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it preserves existing logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Hyperlink Detection**: The HYPERLINK_PATTERN regex remains unchanged[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Anchor Tag Generation**: The code that creates `<a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"url"[0m[39m>name<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m>` remains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintact[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **CSV Parsing**: All core CSV parsing functionality is unaffected[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cell Processing**: Non-hyperlink cells are processed normally[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it addresses the issues:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SSRF Vulnerability**: Completely eliminated by removing all URL connection [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Compilation Errors**: Resolved by removing the method that uses the removed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimports[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Previous Patch Issues**: Completes what the previous patch intended by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremoving the method definition[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential side effects and mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: URLs in HYPERLINK formulas will no longer be fetched and parsed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas embedded documents[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the intended behavior - no tests validate this [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality, and it's inconsistent with how other Tika parsers work[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: The `ExceptionUtils` import is removed[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This import is only used in `processURL` for exception [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling, so it's safe to remove[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: No other methods in the file use EmbeddedDocumentExtractor [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Verification**: The removed imports are only used in `processURL`, confirmed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the compilation errors being localized to that method[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar solutions in the codebase:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe XSSFExcelExtractorDecorator's `extractHyperLinks` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m238[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m250[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovides a reference implementation:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Extracts hyperlinks from Excel files[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Generates anchor tags with href attributes[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does NOT fetch URL content[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does NOT use EmbeddedDocumentExtractor or network classes[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis validates that the proper approach is to generate anchor tags without fetching[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
